Lyrics
Oh Mom!
Look at my thumb,
I've got a booboo,
And fell on my bum.

Oh little baby,
Mom will take care of that,
Put a little plaster,
A pat-a-pat-pat.
Here is your jacket,
And put on your shoe,
Go out and play,
You're as good as new.

Coco...
Look at my toe,
I got a booboo,
From the bathroom door.

Oh little baby,
Coco's here for you,
Give it a rub,
That's what we'll do.
Here is your towel,
Pink and blue,
Go back to bath,
You're as good as new.

Daddy!
Look at my knee,
I got a booboo,
From the swing on the tree,

Oh little baby,
Dad will take care of that,
Put a little plaster,
A pat-a-pat-pat.
Here is your jacket,
And put on your shoe,
Go back to swing,
You're as good as new.

Joey!...
Look at my me,
I got a booboo,
When i swam in the sea.

Oh little baby,
Joey's here for you,
Give it a cleaning,
That's what we'll do.
Here is your flippers,
Purple and blue,
Go back to sea,
You're as good as new.
